info:1 Review

posted:Posted May 3, 2023
msg:5.1 Taking Baoer to Nanjing for fun. I have high requirements for accommodation budget and commuting environment. I chose the holiday inn in Qinhuai after a meal.
First of all, this hotel is far away from the city, so you can have a good sleep at night. Secondly, the price is right. We booked a standard room for 550 two months in advance.
Then the hotel is located inside the Sasseur Outlet (I spent thousands on shopping, which was not in the plan at all, it is really cheap). It is a 5-minute walk to the terminus of Metro Line 3 and can directly reach most attractions such as Confucius Temple.
The front desk of the hotel is on the sixth floor. There is a huge sky garden outside connected to the outlet. There is also a standard basketball court that all guests can use. Across the road, there is a small landscape composed of a small lake and grassland. A plastic track runs for almost 1.5 kilometers.
There are dozens of restaurants in the outlet, as well as a children's playground and a trampoline.
There are many kinds of breakfast, including the signature duck blood vermicelli soup, which is delicious
The room is square and has a bathtub and a microwave.
Finally, I focused on praising the staff for their service. I wrote a handwritten greeting card when I checked in. I prepared a special toothbrush, toothpaste and slippers for my baby. I called to confirm the check-in one day in advance and informed them of the precautions before leaving.

In short, the hotel is recommended to friends who are traveling with children and want to be lively but also want to stay away from the hustle and bustle.
